 '' bharat ratna sachin tendulkar or lata mangeshkar yadi kisi aise samaaroh kaa hissaa hai, jisamen duusare rajya ke mukhyamantri shirkat karne aa rahe hai to phir donon hastiyon kaa protocol mukhyamantri se bhi bada hoga
 If this program is being held in the respective state of the Governor and Chief Minister, then in this situation only the protocol of Sachin Tendulkar and Lata Mangeshkar will be less than them
 darasal, sachin yaa lata mangeshkar hi nahin, bharat ratna se alankrita sabhi vyaktiyon ko bhi vishesh protocol kii suvidha milti he
 In a program outside the states, the protocol of the respective governor and chief minister falls one step short of them, while in the state, the protocol remains one step higher
 is prakaar dekhen to maharashtra ke rajyapal or mukhyamantri ke apane rajya se baahar nikalate hi unka protocol sachin tendulkar or lata mangeshkar ke protocol se kamjor ho jaataa he
 Actually, a preference order has been set by the President's Secretariat for dignitaries and dignitaries sitting in other constitutional positions
 jise teble of presidence kehete hai
 In this, the protocol of posts is fixed for a function
 desh kaa sarvocch sammaan bharat ratna paane vaali hastiyon ko bhi vishesh protocol kii suvidha he
 Such celebrities are placed in the 7-A category of the order of priority of the protocol
 jabaki unase upar raashtrapati(1), uparashtrapati(2), pradhanmantri(3), rajyapal(4), purv raashtrapati(5), uppradhanmantri(6), supreme court ke mukhya nyaayadhish or loksabhaa adhyaksh(6) number par hai, vahiin kendriya mantri, mukhyamantri (apane rajya main), niti ayog ke depyuty chairman, purv pradhanmantri or loksabhaa tathaa rajyasabha ke netaa pratipaksh kaa protocol saatven number par bharat ratna se upar hota he
 Above these, the protocol of the Bharat Ratna Governor and Chief Minister is stronger in their state, while weakening in another state
 teble ko dekhne par pataa chalata he ki agar mukhyamantri apane rajya main he to uskaa protocol saatven number par hota he, vahiin jab vah rajya se baahar hote hai to unka protocol aathven number par hota he
 Similarly, if the Governor is in a function of his state, then his protocol is at number four immediately after the President, Vice President, Prime Minister, but when out of state, his protocol also reaches number eight
 is prakaar yah protocol bharat ratna praapt hastiyon se (7A) se kam hokar aathven number par pahunch jaataa he
 The protocol of the judges of the Supreme Court is also lower than the Bharat Ratna at number eight
 isi tarah sangh lokseva ayog ke chairman, mukhya chunaav ayukta, sieji, rajyasabha or loksabhaa ke depyuty chairman, upmukhyamantri, niti ayog ke sadsy, kendro ke rajya mantri, rajyon ke cabinet mantri, saansadon kaa protocol bhi bharat ratna alankrita vyaktiyon se kamjor hota he
 In the Table of Presidency issued by the President's Secretariat, it has been said that this preference has been fixed only for ceremonies

 rawalpindi sthit adaalat ne kaha ki musharraf ko aaj kii sunwaayee main hi yahaan nyaayadhish ke samaksh pesh karnaa chahie tha, lekin suraksha kaarnon se aisa nahin ho sakaa
 Federal Investigation Agency (FIA) Chief Prosecutor Zulfiqar Ali has given this information
 adaalat ne 69 saal ke musharraf ko bhale hi 14 dinon ke liye nyaayik hiraasat main bheja he, lekin vah islamabad ke bahari ilaake chak shahzad sthit apane farmahouse main rahenge

 tippaniyan Regarding the fia's decision not to produce Musharraf in court today, Chief Prosecutor Zulfiqar Ali told reporters that the Home Ministry issued an order stating that the former president faces a very high level of security risk
